<p>The native input file element is quite difficult to style and doesn&#x27;t provide a
drag-n-drop version.</p>
<blockquote class="my_5 px_4 py_3 bg_bg.tertiary.subtle bd-w_1px bd-l-c_border.primary.subtle bd-l-w_2px bdr_4px bd-c_border">
<p>The file upload component doesn&#x27;t handle the actual file uploading process. It
only handles the UI and the state of the file upload.</p>
</blockquote>

<p><strong>Features</strong></p>
<ul>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted">Supports a button to open the file dialog</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted">Supports drag and drop to upload files</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted">Set the maximum number of files that can be uploaded</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted">Set the maximum size of the files that can be uploaded</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted">Set the accepted file types</li>
</ul>

<h2 id="anatomy" class="textStyle_display.md mt_12 mb_3">Anatomy<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#anatomy"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h2>
<p>To set up the file upload correctly, you&#x27;ll need to understand its anatomy and
how we name its parts.</p>
<blockquote class="my_5 px_4 py_3 bg_bg.tertiary.subtle bd-w_1px bd-l-c_border.primary.subtle bd-l-w_2px bdr_4px bd-c_border">
<p>Each part includes a <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">data-part</code> attribute to help identify them in the DOM.</p>
</blockquote>

<h2 id="usage" class="textStyle_display.md mt_12 mb_3">Usage<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#usage"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h2>
<p>Import the file upload package:</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword module">import</span> <span class="token imports"><span class="token operator">*</span> <span class="token keyword module">as</span> fileUpload</span> <span class="token keyword module">from</span> <span class="token string">&quot;@zag-js/file-upload&quot;</span>
</span></div></pre>
<p>The file upload package exports two key functions:</p>
<ul>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted"><code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">machine</code> - Behavior logic.</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted"><code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">connect</code> - Maps behavior to JSX props and event handlers.</li>
</ul>
<p>Then use the framework integration helpers:</p>
<div data-scope="tabs" data-part="root" id="tabs:file-upload/usage.mdx" data-orientation="horizontal" dir="ltr" class="w_full max-w_768px bd-w_1px my_8 bg_bg.code.block bdr_6px"><div data-scope="tabs" </span><span class="code-line">      <span class="token tag"><span class="token tag"><span class="token punctuation">&lt;</span>li</span>
</span></span><span class="code-line"><span class="token tag">        <span class="token attr-name">v-for</span><span class="token attr-value"><span class="token punctuation attr-equals">=</span><span class="token punctuation">&quot;</span>file in api.acceptedFiles<span class="token punctuation">&quot;</span></span>
</span></span><span class="code-line"><span class="token tag">        <span class="token attr-name">:key</span><span class="token attr-value"><span class="token punctuation attr-equals">=</span><span class="token punctuation">&quot;</span>file.name<span class="token punctuation">&quot;</span></span>
</span></span><span class="code-line"><span class="token tag">        <span class="token attr-name">v-bind</span><span class="token attr-value"><span class="token punctuation attr-equals">=</span><span class="token punctuation">&quot;</span>api.getItemProps({ file })<span class="token punctuation">&quot;</span></span>

<h3 id="setting-the-accepted-file-types" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Setting the accepted file types<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#setting-the-accepted-file-types"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>Use the <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">accept</code> attribute to set the accepted file types.</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>fileUpload<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">accept</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">&quot;image/*&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<p>Alternatively, you can provide an object with a MIME type and an array of file
extensions.</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>fileUpload<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">accept</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token string-property property">&quot;image/png&quot;</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token string">&quot;.png&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token string-property property">&quot;text/html&quot;</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token string">&quot;.html&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token string">&quot;.htm&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="setting-the-maximum-number-of-files" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Setting the maximum number of files<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#setting-the-maximum-number-of-files"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>Use <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">maxFiles</code> to set how many files can be selected.</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>fileUpload<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">maxFiles</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token number">5</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="setting-the-minimum-size-per-file" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Setting the minimum size per file<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#setting-the-minimum-size-per-file"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>Use <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">minFileSize</code> to reject files smaller than a minimum size.</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>fileUpload<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">minFileSize</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token number">1024</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token comment">// 1KB</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="setting-the-maximum-size-per-file" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Setting the maximum size per file<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#setting-the-maximum-size-per-file"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>Use the <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">maxFileSize</code> attribute to set the maximum size per file that can be
uploaded.</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>fileUpload<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">maxFileSize</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token number">1024</span> <span class="token operator">*</span> <span class="token number">1024</span> <span class="token operator">*</span> <span class="token number">10</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token comment">// 10MB</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="setting-initial-files" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Setting initial files<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#setting-initial-files"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>Use <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">defaultAcceptedFiles</code> to prefill the accepted files list.</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>fileUpload<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">defaultAcceptedFiles</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token punctuation">[</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token keyword">new</span> <span class="token class-name">File</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token string">&quot;hello&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token string">&quot;hello.txt&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span> <span class="token literal-property property">type</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">&quot;text/plain&quot;</span> <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token punctuation">]</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="controlled-files" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Controlled files<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#controlled-files"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>Use <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">acceptedFiles</code> and <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">onFileChange</code> to control accepted files externally.</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>fileUpload<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  acceptedFiles<span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token function">onFileChange</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token parameter">details</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token function">setAcceptedFiles</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>details<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">acceptedFiles</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="listening-to-file-changes" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Listening to file changes<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#listening-to-file-changes"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>When files are uploaded, the <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">onFileChange</code> callback is invoked with the details
of the accepted and rejected files.</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>fileUpload<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token function">onFileChange</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token parameter">details</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token comment">// details =&gt; { acceptedFiles: File[], rejectedFiles: { file: File, errors: FileError[] }[] }</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token console class-name">console</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">log</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>details<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">acceptedFiles</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token console class-name">console</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">log</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>details<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">rejectedFiles</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="listening-to-accept-and-reject-events" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Listening to accept and reject events<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#listening-to-accept-and-reject-events"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>Use <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">onFileAccept</code> and <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">onFileReject</code> for separated success/failure flows.</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>fileUpload<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token function">onFileAccept</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token parameter">details</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token console class-name">console</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">log</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">&quot;Accepted:&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> details<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">files</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token function">onFileReject</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token parameter">details</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token console class-name">console</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">log</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">&quot;Rejected:&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> details<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">files</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="usage-within-a-form" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Usage within a form<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#usage-within-a-form"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>To use file upload in a form, set <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">name</code> and render <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">api.getHiddenInputProps()</code>.</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>fileUpload<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">name</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">&quot;avatar&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token tag"><span class="token tag"><span class="token punctuation">&lt;</span>input</span> <span class="token spread"><span class="token punctuation">{</span><span class="token spread operator">...</span>api<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">getHiddenInputProps</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">}</span></span> <span class="token punctuation">/&gt;</span></span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="displaying-image-preview" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Displaying image preview<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#displaying-image-preview"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>To display a preview of the uploaded image, use the built-in FileReader API to
read the file and set the <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">src</code> attribute of an image element.</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>fileUpload<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token function">onFileChange</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token parameter">details</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token keyword">const</span> reader <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token keyword">new</span> <span class="token class-name">FileReader</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    reader<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method-variable function-variable method function property-access">onload</span> <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token parameter">event</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token arrow operator">=&gt;</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">      <span class="token keyword">const</span> image <span class="token operator">=</span> event<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">target</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">result</span>
</span><span class="code-line">      <span class="token comment">// set the image as the src of an image element</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    reader<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">readAsDataURL</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>details<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">acceptedFiles</span><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token number">0</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="applying-custom-validation" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Applying custom validation<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#applying-custom-validation"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>To apply custom validation, set <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">validate</code> to a function that returns an <strong>array
of error strings</strong>.</p>
<p>The returned array can contain any string as an error message. While zagjs
supports default errors such as <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">TOO_MANY_FILES</code>, <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">FILE_INVALID_TYPE</code>,
<code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">FILE_TOO_LARGE</code>, or <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">FILE_TOO_SMALL</code>, you can return any string that represents
your custom validation errors.</p>
<blockquote class="my_5 px_4 py_3 bg_bg.tertiary.subtle bd-w_1px bd-l-c_border.primary.subtle bd-l-w_2px bdr_4px bd-c_border">
<p>Return <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">null</code> if no validation errors are detected.</p>
</blockquote>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>fileUpload<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token function">validate</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token parameter">file<span class="token punctuation">,</span> details</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token comment">// Check if file size exceeds 10MB</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token keyword control-flow">if</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span>file<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">size</span> <span class="token operator">&gt;</span> <span class="token number">1024</span> <span class="token operator">*</span> <span class="token number">1024</span> <span class="token operator">*</span> <span class="token number">10</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">      <span class="token keyword control-flow">return</span> <span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token string">&quot;FILE_TOO_LARGE&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token comment">// details =&gt; { acceptedFiles, rejectedFiles }</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token console class-name">console</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">log</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>details<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">acceptedFiles</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">length</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token keyword control-flow">return</span> <span class="token keyword null nil">null</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<p>Apply multiple validation errors:</p>
<pre class="prose language-js"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>fileUpload<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token function">validate</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token parameter">file<span class="token punctuation">,</span> details</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token keyword">const</span> errors <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span>
</span><span class="code-line">
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token comment">// Check file size</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token keyword control-flow">if</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span>file<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">size</span> <span class="token operator">&gt;</span> <span class="token number">10</span> <span class="token operator">*</span> <span class="token number">1024</span> <span class="token operator">*</span> <span class="token number">1024</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">      errors<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">push</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">&quot;FILE_TOO_LARGE&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token comment">// Default error enum</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span><span class="code-line">
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token comment">// Ensure file is a PDF</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token keyword control-flow">if</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token operator">!</span>file<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">name</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">endsWith</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">&quot;.pdf&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">      errors<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">push</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">&quot;ONLY_PDF_ALLOWED&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token comment">// Custom error</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span><span class="code-line">
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token comment">// Custom check: Reject duplicate files</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token keyword">const</span> isDuplicate <span class="token operator">=</span> details<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">acceptedFiles</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">some</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>
</span><span class="code-line">      <span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token parameter">acceptedFile</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token arrow operator">=&gt;</span> acceptedFile<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">name</span> <span class="token operator">===</span> file<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">name</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token keyword control-flow">if</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span>isDuplicate<span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">      errors<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">push</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">&quot;FILE_EXISTS&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span><span class="code-line">
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token keyword control-flow">return</span> errors<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">length</span> <span class="token operator">&gt;</span> <span class="token number">0</span> <span class="token operator">?</span> errors <span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token keyword null nil">null</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="disabling-drag-and-drop" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Disabling drag and drop<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#disabling-drag-and-drop"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>Set <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">allowDrop</code> to <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">false</code> to disable drag and drop.</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>fileUpload<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">allowDrop</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token boolean">false</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="preventing-document-level-drop" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Preventing document-level drop<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#preventing-document-level-drop"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>Set <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">preventDocumentDrop</code> to <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">false</code> if you do not want this component to block
file drops outside the dropzone.</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>fileUpload<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">preventDocumentDrop</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token boolean">false</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="read-only-mode" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Read-only mode<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#read-only-mode"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>Set <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">readOnly</code> to prevent adding or removing files.</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>fileUpload<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">readOnly</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token boolean">true</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="allowing-directory-selection" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Allowing directory selection<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#allowing-directory-selection"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>Set the <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">directory</code> property to <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">true</code> to enable selecting directories instead
of files.</p>
<p>This maps to the native input <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">webkitdirectory</code> HTML attribute and allows users
to select directories and their contents.</p>
<blockquote class="my_5 px_4 py_3 bg_bg.tertiary.subtle bd-w_1px bd-l-c_border.primary.subtle bd-l-w_2px bdr_4px bd-c_border">
<p>Please note that support for this feature varies from browser to browser.</p>
</blockquote>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>fileUpload<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">directory</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token boolean">true</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="supporting-media-capture-on-mobile-devices" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Supporting media capture on mobile devices<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#supporting-media-capture-on-mobile-devices"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>Set the <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">capture</code> property to specify the media capture mechanism to capture
media on the spot. The value can be:</p>
<ul>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted"><code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">user</code> for capturing media from the user-facing camera</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted"><code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">environment</code> for the outward-facing camera</li>
</ul>
<blockquote class="my_5 px_4 py_3 bg_bg.tertiary.subtle bd-w_1px bd-l-c_border.primary.subtle bd-l-w_2px bdr_4px bd-c_border">
<p>This behavior only works on mobile devices. On desktop devices, it will open
the file system like normal.</p>
</blockquote>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>fileUpload<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">capture</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">&quot;user&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="pasting-files-from-clipboard" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Pasting files from clipboard<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#pasting-files-from-clipboard"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>After a user copies an image, to allow pasting the files from the clipboard, you
can listen for the paste event and use the <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">api.setFiles</code> method to set the
files.</p>
<p>Here&#x27;s an example of how to do this in React.</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">function</span> <span class="token function"><span class="token maybe-class-name">Demo</span></span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>fileUpload<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token literal-property property">accept</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">&quot;image/*&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line">
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token keyword">const</span> api <span class="token operator">=</span> fileUpload<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">connect</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>service<span class="token punctuation">,</span> normalizeProps<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line">
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token keyword control-flow">return</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token tag"><span class="token tag"><span class="token punctuation">&lt;</span>textarea</span>
</span></span><span class="code-line"><span class="token tag">      <span class="token attr-name">onPaste</span><span class="token script language-javascript"><span class="token script-punctuation punctuation">=</span><span class="token punctuation">{</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token parameter">event</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token arrow operator">=&gt;</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span></span></span><span class="code-line"><span class="token tag"><span class="token script language-javascript">        <span class="token keyword control-flow">if</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span>event<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">clipboardData</span><span class="token operator">?.</span>files<span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span></span></span><span class="code-line"><span class="token tag"><span class="token script language-javascript">          api<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">setFiles</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token known-class-name class-name">Array</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token keyword module">from</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>event<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">clipboardData</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">files</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></span></span><span class="code-line"><span class="token tag"><span class="token script language-javascript">        <span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span></span></span><span class="code-line"><span class="token tag"><span class="token script language-javascript">      <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">}</span></span>
</span></span><span class="code-line"><span class="token tag">    <span class="token punctuation">/&gt;</span></span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="transforming-files-before-acceptance" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Transforming files before acceptance<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#transforming-files-before-acceptance"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>Use the <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">transformFiles</code> callback to process files before they&#x27;re added to
<code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">acceptedFiles</code>. This is useful for scenarios like image cropping, compression,
or format conversion.</p>
<p>The <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">transformFiles</code> function receives the selected files and should return a
promise that resolves with the transformed files.</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>fileUpload<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">accept</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">&quot;image/*&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token function-variable function">transformFiles</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token keyword">async</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token parameter">files</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token arrow operator">=&gt;</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token keyword control-flow">return</span> <span class="token known-class-name class-name">Promise</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">all</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>
</span><span class="code-line">      files<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">map</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token keyword">async</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token parameter">file</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token arrow operator">=&gt;</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">        <span class="token comment">// Compress or transform the file</span>
</span><span class="code-line">        <span class="token keyword">const</span> transformedBlob <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token keyword control-flow">await</span> <span class="token function">processImage</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>file<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line">        <span class="token keyword control-flow">return</span> <span class="token keyword">new</span> <span class="token class-name">File</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">[</span>transformedBlob<span class="token punctuation">]</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> file<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">name</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span> <span class="token literal-property property">type</span><span class="token operator">:</span> file<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">type</span> <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line">      <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<p>While files are being transformed, the <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">api.transforming</code> boolean is <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">true</code>,
allowing you to show loading states in your UI.</p>
<h3 id="customizing-accessibility-labels" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Customizing accessibility labels<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#customizing-accessibility-labels"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>Use <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">translations</code> to customize dropzone and item action labels.</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>fileUpload<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">translations</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token literal-property property">dropzone</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">&quot;Drop files here&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token function-variable function">deleteFile</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token parameter">file</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token arrow operator">=&gt;</span> <span class="token template-string"><span class="token template-punctuation string">`</span><span class="token string">Remove </span><span class="token interpolation"><span class="token interpolation-punctuation punctuation">${</span>file<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">name</span><span class="token interpolation-punctuation punctuation">}</span></span><span class="token template-punctuation string">`</span></span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h2 id="styling-guide" class="textStyle_display.md mt_12 mb_3">Styling guide<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#styling-guide"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h2>
<p>Each part includes a <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">data-part</code> attribute you can target in CSS.</p>
<pre class="prose language-css"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token selector"><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-part</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;root&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span></span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token comment">/* styles for root element*/</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span><span class="code-line">
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token selector"><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-part</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;dropzone&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span></span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token comment">/* styles for root element*/</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span><span class="code-line">
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token selector"><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-part</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;trigger&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span></span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token comment">/* styles for file picker trigger */</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span><span class="code-line">
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token selector"><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-part</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;label&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span></span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token comment">/* styles for the input&#x27;s label */</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="dragging-state" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Dragging State<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#dragging-state"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>When the user drags a file over the file upload, the <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">data-dragging</code> attribute
is added to the <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">root</code> and <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">dropzone</code> parts.</p>
<pre class="prose language-css"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token selector"><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-part</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;root&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-dragging</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span></span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token comment">/* styles for when the user is dragging a file over the file upload */</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span><span class="code-line">
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token selector"><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-part</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;dropzone&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-dragging</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span></span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token comment">/* styles for when the user is dragging a file over the file upload */</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="disabled-state" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Disabled State<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#disabled-state"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>When the file upload is disabled, the <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">data-disabled</code> attribute is added to the
component parts.</p>
<pre class="prose language-css"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token selector"><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-part</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;root&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-disabled</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span></span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token comment">/* styles for when the file upload is disabled */</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span><span class="code-line">
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token selector"><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-part</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;dropzone&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-disabled</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span></span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token comment">/* styles for when the file upload is disabled */</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span><span class="code-line">
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token selector"><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-part</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;trigger&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-disabled</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span></span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token comment">/* styles for when the file upload is disabled */</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span><span class="code-line">
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token selector"><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-part</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;label&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-disabled</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span></span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token comment">/* styles for when the file upload is disabled */</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h2 id="methods-and-properties" class="textStyle_display.md mt_12 mb_3">Methods and Properties<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#methods-and-properties"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h2>
<h3 id="machine-context" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Machine Context<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#machine-context"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>The file upload machine exposes the following context properties:</p>
<ul class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 pl_0! li-t_none dvd-y_1px li-pos_inside"><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">name</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">string</code><span class="d_block">The name of the underlying file input</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">ids</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">Partial&lt;{ root: string; dropzone: string; hiddenInput: string; trigger: string; label: string; item: (id: string) =&gt; string; itemName: (id: string) =&gt; string; itemSizeText: (id: string) =&gt; string; itemPreview: (id: string) =&gt; string; itemDeleteTrigger: (id: string) =&gt; string; }&gt;</code><span class="d_block">The ids of the elements. <h3 id="machine-api" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Machine API<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#machine-api"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>The file upload <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">api</code> exposes the following methods:</p>

file upload component lets users select and manage files.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eThe native input file element is quite difficult to style and doesn't provide a\ndrag-n-drop version.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cblockquote\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eThe file upload component doesn't handle the actual file uploading process. It\nonly handles the UI and the state of the file upload.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003c/blockquote\u003e\n\u003cresources pkg=\"@zag-js/file-upload\"\u003e\n\u003cshowcase package:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-jsx\"\u003eimport * as fileUpload from \"@zag-js/file-upload\"\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eThe file upload package exports two key functions:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cul\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003emachine\u003c/code\u003e - Behavior logic.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003econnect\u003c/code\u003e - Maps behavior to JSX props and event handlers.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eThen use the framework integration helpers:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003ccodesnippet id=\"file-upload/usage.mdx\"\u003e\n\u003ch3\u003eSetting the accepted file types\u003c/h3\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eUse the \u003ccode\u003eaccept\u003c/code\u003e attribute to set the accepted file types.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-jsx\"\u003econst service = useMachine(fileUpload.machine, {\n  accept: \"image/*\",\n})\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eAlternatively, you can provide an object with a MIME type and an array of file\nextensions.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-jsx\"\u003econst service = useMachine(fileUpload.machine, {\n  accept: {\n    \"image/png\": [\".png\"],\n    \"text/html\": [\".html\", \".htm\"],\n  },\n})\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003ch3\u003eSetting the maximum number of files\u003c/h3\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eUse \u003ccode\u003emaxFiles\u003c/code\u003e to set how many files can be selected.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-jsx\"\u003econst service = useMachine(fileUpload.machine, {\n  maxFiles: 5,\n})\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003ch3\u003eSetting the minimum size per file\u003c/h3\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eUse \u003ccode\u003eminFileSize\u003c/code\u003e to reject files smaller than a minimum size.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-jsx\"\u003econst service = useMachine(fileUpload.machine, {\n  minFileSize: 1024, // 1KB\n})\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003ch3\u003eSetting the maximum size per file\u003c/h3\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eUse the \u003ccode\u003emaxFileSize\u003c/code\u003e attribute to set the maximum size per file that can be\nuploaded.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-jsx\"\u003econst service = useMachine(fileUpload.machine, {\n  maxFileSize: 1024 * 1024 * 10, // 10MB\n})\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003ch3\u003eSetting initial files\u003c/h3\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eUse \u003ccode\u003edefaultAcceptedFiles\u003c/code\u003e to prefill the accepted files list.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-jsx\"\u003econst service = useMachine(fileUpload.machine, {\n  defaultAcceptedFiles: [\n    new File([\"hello\"], \"hello.txt\", { type: \"text/plain\" }),\n  ],\n})\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003ch3\u003eControlled files\u003c/h3\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eUse \u003ccode\u003eacceptedFiles\u003c/code\u003e and \u003ccode\u003eonFileChange\u003c/code\u003e to control accepted files externally.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-jsx\"\u003econst service = useMachine(fileUpload.machine, {\n  acceptedFiles,\n  onFileChange(details) {\n    setAcceptedFiles(details.acceptedFiles)\n  },\n})\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003ch3\u003eListening to file changes\u003c/h3\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eWhen files are uploaded, the \u003ccode\u003eonFileChange\u003c/code\u003e callback is invoked with the details\nof the accepted and rejected files.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-jsx\"\u003econst service = useMachine(fileUpload.machine, {\n  onFileChange(details) {\n    // details =\u003e { acceptedFiles: File[], rejectedFiles: { file: File, errors: FileError[] }[] }\n    console.log(details.acceptedFiles)\n    console.log(details.rejectedFiles)\n  },\n})\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003ch3\u003eListening to accept and reject events\u003c/h3\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eUse \u003ccode\u003eonFileAccept\u003c/code\u003e and \u003ccode\u003eonFileReject\u003c/code\u003e for separated success/failure flows.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-jsx\"\u003econst service = useMachine(fileUpload.machine, {\n  onFileAccept(details) {\n    console.log(\"Accepted:\", details.files)\n  },\n  onFileReject(details) {\n    console.log(\"Rejected:\", details.files)\n  },\n})\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003ch3\u003eUsage within a form\u003c/h3\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eTo use file upload in a form, set \u003ccode\u003ename\u003c/code\u003e and render \u003ccode\u003eapi.getHiddenInputProps()\u003c/code\u003e.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-jsx\"\u003econst service = useMachine(fileUpload.machine, {\n  name: \"avatar\",\n})\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-jsx\"\u003e\u0026#x3C;input {...api.getHiddenInputProps()} /\u003e\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003ch3\u003eDisplaying image preview\u003c/h3\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eTo display a preview of the uploaded image, use the built-in FileReader API to\nread the file and set the \u003ccode\u003esrc\u003c/code\u003e attribute of an image element.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-jsx\"\u003econst service = useMachine(fileUpload.machine, {\n  onFileChange(details) {\n    const reader = new FileReader()\n    reader.onload = (event) =\u003e {\n      const image = event.target.result\n      // set the image as the src of an image element\n    }\n    reader.readAsDataURL(details.acceptedFiles[0])\n  },\n})\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003ch3\u003eApplying custom validation\u003c/h3\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eTo apply custom validation, set \u003ccode\u003evalidate\u003c/code\u003e to a function that returns an \u003cstrong\u003earray\nof error strings\u003c/strong\u003e.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eThe returned array can contain any string as an error message. While zagjs\nsupports default errors such as \u003ccode\u003eTOO_MANY_FILES\u003c/code\u003e, \u003ccode\u003eFILE_INVALID_TYPE\u003c/code\u003e,\n\u003ccode\u003eFILE_TOO_LARGE\u003c/code\u003e, or \u003ccode\u003eFILE_TOO_SMALL\u003c/code\u003e, you can return any string that represents\nyour custom validation errors.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cblockquote\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eReturn \u003ccode\u003enull\u003c/code\u003e if no validation errors are detected.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003c/blockquote\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-jsx\"\u003econst service = useMachine(fileUpload.machine, {\n  validate(file, details) {\n    // Check if file size exceeds 10MB\n    if (file.size \u003e 1024 * 1024 * 10) {\n      return [\"FILE_TOO_LARGE\"]\n    }\n    // details =\u003e { acceptedFiles, rejectedFiles }\n    console.log(details.acceptedFiles.length)\n    return null\n  },\n})\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eApply multiple validation errors:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-js\"\u003econst service = useMachine(fileUpload.machine, {\n  validate(file, details) {\n    const errors = []\n\n    // Check file size\n    if (file.size \u003e 10 * 1024 * 1024) {\n      errors.push(\"FILE_TOO_LARGE\") // Default error enum\n    }\n\n    // Ensure file is a PDF\n    if (!file.name.endsWith(\".pdf\")) {\n      errors.push(\"ONLY_PDF_ALLOWED\") // Custom error\n    }\n\n    // Custom check: Reject duplicate files\n    const isDuplicate = details.acceptedFiles.some(\n      (acceptedFile) =\u003e acceptedFile.name === file.name,\n    )\n    if (isDuplicate) {\n      errors.push(\"FILE_EXISTS\")\n    }\n\n    return errors.length \u003e 0 ? errors : null\n  },\n})\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003ch3\u003eDisabling drag and drop\u003c/h3\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eSet \u003ccode\u003eallowDrop\u003c/code\u003e to \u003ccode\u003efalse\u003c/code\u003e to disable drag and drop.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-jsx\"\u003econst service = useMachine(fileUpload.machine, {\n  allowDrop: false,\n})\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003ch3\u003ePreventing document-level drop\u003c/h3\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eSet \u003ccode\u003epreventDocumentDrop\u003c/code\u003e to \u003ccode\u003efalse\u003c/code\u003e if you do not want this component to block\nfile drops outside the dropzone.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-jsx\"\u003econst service = useMachine(fileUpload.machine, {\n  preventDocumentDrop: false,\n})\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003ch3\u003eRead-only mode\u003c/h3\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eSet \u003ccode\u003ereadOnly\u003c/code\u003e to prevent adding or removing files.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-jsx\"\u003econst service = useMachine(fileUpload.machine, {\n  readOnly: true,\n})\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003ch3\u003eAllowing directory selection\u003c/h3\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eSet the \u003ccode\u003edirectory\u003c/code\u003e property to \u003ccode\u003etrue\u003c/code\u003e to enable selecting directories instead\nof files.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eThis maps to the native input \u003ccode\u003ewebkitdirectory\u003c/code\u003e HTML
